aria-label="Donald Trump"\n                                        \n                                    style="background-image: </div></div>\n                            \n                </div><div class="widget__body clearfix sm-mt-1"><div class="photo-credit">\n        Official White House Photo by Tia Dufour\n    </div><span class="js-scroll-trigger" data-target="body" data-triggers="render-rebelbar" data-toggle-class="with-floating-shares"></span>\n<div id="utm_campaign"></div><div class="body js-expandable clearfix js-listicle-body js-update-url css-listicle-body-2648125982"\n        \n            data-elid="2648125982"\n            data-post-url="https://www.nationalmemo.com/trump-seems-badly-confused-as-he-quits-relief-talks"\n            \n                data-authors="Cody Fenwick"\n            \n            \n                data-headline="Trump Seems Badly Confused As He Quits Coronavirus Relief Talks"\n            \n        ><div class="body-description" ><div class="inarticle_ad_placeholder" data-aa-adunit="/5931858/NatMemo_RM/NatMemo_Middle_Desktop_1" data-aaad="true"></div>\n<!--script id="3d14008d7e044c36b256c61ff82728bb">\nif(cnxFlag){\n\n  cnx.cmd.push(function() {\n    cnx({\n      playerId: \'5573e7ba-804a-4971-a00f-3e2eeec6c0a9\'\n    }).render(\'3d14008d7e044c36b256c61ff82728bb\');\n  });\ncnxFlag=false;\n}\n</script--><p><em>Reprinted with permission from <a href="https://www.alternet.org/2020/10/trumps-one-word-tweet-made-people-question-his-mental-health-heres-what-seems-to-be-going-on/" target="_blank">Alternet</a></em></p><p>As President Donald Trump continues the struggle to recover from his case of COVID-19, he sent entirely mixed messages on Tuesday that left some questioning whether he retained full control of his faculties.</p><p>First, <a href="https://www.alternet.org/2020/10/trump-just-torpedoed-his-best-hope-for-re-election/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Trump torpedoed negotiations with congressional Democrats</a> over a potential stimulus bill on Tuesday afternoon, saying that he would wait until after the election until trying again. This was a major blow to his own hopes for re-election, but the move itself could be coherently explained on ideological or tactical grounds, even if they\'re not compelling or persuasive.</p><hr/><p>But just a few hours later, he seemed to completely reverse himself in a one-word tweet:</p><script id="3d14008d7e044c36b256c61ff82728bb">\nif(cnxFlag){\ncnxFlag=false;\n  cnx.cmd.push(function() {\n    cnx({\n      playerId: \'5573e7ba-804a-4971-a00f-3e2eeec6c0a9\'\n    }).render(\'3d14008d7e044c36b256c61ff82728bb\');\n  });\n}\n</script><div class="rm-shortcode" data-rm-shortcode-id="427015de96c2aabcd2af678bcd8db9bc" id="99fdb"><blockquote class="twitter-tweet twitter-custom-tweet" data-partner="rebelmouse" data-twitter-tweet-id="1313615182535499779"><div style="margin:1em 0">True! https://t.co/ZJmcxG2CoO</div> \xe2\x80\x94 Donald J. Trump (@Donald J. Trump)<a href="https://twitter.com/realDonaldTrump/statuses/1313615182535499779">1602025239.0</a></blockquote></div><p>Here\'s the big problem with this tweet: Trump had just rejected Congress\'s efforts to provide help to the economy that Fed Chair Jerome Powell is advocating in the tweet that he is calling "True!" Not only that, he\'s rejecting the congressional help for precisely the reasons Powell said \xe2\x80\x94 in that very tweet \xe2\x80\x94 that we shouldn\'t be concerned with. Trump blasted House Speaker Nancy Pelosi for asking for too much money. But that\'s exactly what Powell says shouldn\'t matter \xe2\x80\x94 "there\'s a low risk of \'overdoing it,\'" as the tweet said.</p><div class="inarticle_ad_placeholder" data-aa-adunit="/5931858/NatMemo_RM/NatMemo_Middle_Desktop_2" data-aaad="true"></div>\n<div class="video-container" id="videoCont" style="display: none;"></div>\n<div id="vid"></div><p><br/></p><div class="rm-shortcode" data-rm-shortcode-id="095bb64673709ddaedf385756d8c18c7" id="93915"><blockquote class="twitter-tweet twitter-custom-tweet" data-partner="rebelmouse" data-twitter-tweet-id="1313551794623127552"><div style="margin:1em 0">Nancy Pelosi is asking for $2.4 Trillion\xc2\xa0Dollars\xc2\xa0to bailout poorly run, high crime, Democrat States, money that is\xe2\x80\xa6 https://t.co/PteAZiyD9S</div> \xe2\x80\x94 Donald J. Trump (@Donald J. Trump)<a href="https://twitter.com/realDonaldTrump/statuses/1313551794623127552">1602010127.0</a></blockquote></div><p>People responded to the one-word Trump tweet with bafflement and dismay about the president\'s mental condition.<br/></p><p><br/></p><p><br/></p><div class="rm-shortcode" data-rm-shortcode-id="ac61cfbb1efdecbfbb5282935ae600ea" id="5e1d4"><blockquote class="twitter-tweet twitter-custom-tweet" data-partner="rebelmouse" data-twitter-tweet-id="1313620712666656768"><div style="margin:1em 0">I wonder if Trump could do the Person. Man. Woman. TV. Camera thing. He seems to have forgotten sending the stock m\xe2\x80\xa6 https://t.co/SsDFuGINqt</div> \xe2\x80\x94 Jennifer \'Vote Early\' Rubin (@Jennifer \'Vote Early\' Rubin)<a href="https://twitter.com/JRubinBlogger/statuses/1313620712666656768">1602026558.0</a></blockquote></div><p><br/></p><div class="rm-shortcode" data-rm-shortcode-id="97b950924d57111859a38f555fe38613" id="7b849"><blockquote class="twitter-tweet twitter-custom-tweet" data-partner="rebelmouse" data-twitter-tweet-id="1313621749267927045"><div style="margin:1em 0">??? https://t.co/1UHbxyZe2m</div> \xe2\x80\x94 Jeff Stein (@Jeff Stein)<a href="https://twitter.com/JStein_WaPo/statuses/1313621749267927045">1602026805.0</a></blockquote></div><p><br/></p><div class="rm-shortcode" data-rm-shortcode-id="8a073fd110b138154165d22a62559056" id="27843"><blockquote class="twitter-tweet twitter-custom-tweet" data-partner="rebelmouse" data-twitter-tweet-id="1313619189496713218"><div style="margin:1em 0">Who\'s tweeting from the President\'s account? Who knows? Is the President well enough and sufficiently of sound mind\xe2\x80\xa6 https://t.co/mz3vjzdGv5</div> \xe2\x80\x94 Chris Hayes (@Chris Hayes)<a href="https://twitter.com/chrislhayes/statuses/1313619189496713218">1602026195.0</a></blockquote></div><p><br/></p><div class="rm-shortcode" data-rm-shortcode-id="5ea24f21249b5971e18fd8a943449fcb" id="ed2f8"><blockquote class="twitter-tweet twitter-custom-tweet" data-partner="rebelmouse" data-twitter-tweet-id="1313618365337001995"><div style="margin:1em 0">been staring at this for like five minutes now trying to understand what he could possibly think those words mean https://t.co/hNnQZHqU2k</div> \xe2\x80\x94 Ashley Feinberg (@Ashley Feinberg)<a href="https://twitter.com/ashleyfeinberg/statuses/1313618365337001995">1602025998.0</a></blockquote></div><p><br/></p><div class="rm-shortcode" data-rm-shortcode-id="0ff6ce6b794900ef08a8870c8ee6907d" id="a6ac7"><blockquote class="twitter-tweet twitter-custom-tweet" data-partner="rebelmouse" data-twitter-tweet-id="1313618510657052676"><div style="margin:1em 0">Seriously, one has to wonder about his cognition. This is not normal, even for him.</div> \xe2\x80\x94 Seth Hanlon (@Seth Hanlon)<a href="https://twitter.com/SethHanlon/statuses/1313618510657052676">1602026033.0</a></blockquote></div><p>It\'s easy to make jokes about, but it\'s actually not funny at all and is genuinely concerning. The president is still battling COVID-19, a brutal infection that can take a serious toll on the mind and body. This along has led to some to suggest he cede power to Vice President Mike Pence until he is out of the woods. On top of that, the president is taking a group of drugs to treat his disease, including a steroid that has potential effects mood. Again, we don\'t want to be glib about this. It\'s very serious, and the president shouldn\'t be accused of mental instability easily or out of pure partisan sniping. But it was hard to make sense of the president\'s incongruous opinions on the highly significant matter before him: potentially trillions of dollars of economic recovery funds.</p><p><a href="https://twitter.com/HayesBrown/status/1313621914133434368" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Hayes Brown</a> of <em>BuzzFeed</em> suggested that Trump\'s point could make sense if you "remember that Trump was always pushing the GOP to spend more. It wasn\'t about the bill being too big, it was that he didn\'t want money spent anywhere that it might help Democrats, like in big cities or blue states." And that interpretation was bolstered by a subsequent tweet, sent about forty minutes later:</p><p><br/></p><div class="rm-shortcode" data-rm-shortcode-id="2c6aac4132453708aa05a23e9e5184f0" id="4c6f1"><blockquote class="twitter-tweet twitter-custom-tweet" data-partner="rebelmouse" data-twitter-tweet-id="1313624267842560000"><div style="margin:1em 0">Crazy Nancy Pelosi and the Radical Left Democrats were just playing \xe2\x80\x9cgames\xe2\x80\x9d with the desperately needed Workers Sti\xe2\x80\xa6 https://t.co/gnPNISrcIs</div> \xe2\x80\x94 Donald J. Trump (@Donald J. Trump)<a href="https://twitter.com/realDonaldTrump/statuses/1313624267842560000">1602027406.0</a></blockquote></div><p>Even so, the explanation still doesn\'t make much sense. Even on this reading, Trump clearly didn\'t get Powell\'s point, which is that we should be willing to spend a lot of money to support the economy and that the costs of delay or insufficient spending are worse than the possibility of waste. And this interpretation doesn\'t completely erase concerns about his mental condition, because he genuinely seems unable or unwilling to grasp Powell\'s point. But this may just reflect Trump\'s more typical, if still deeply concerning, way of processing and conveying information.<br/></p><div class="inarticle_ad_placeholder" data-aa-adunit="/5931858/NatMemo_RM/NatMemo_Middle_Desktop_3" data-aaad="true"></div><p>Brandon Wall, also of <em>BuzzFeed News</em>, agreed with Brown\'s reading, saying: "Yes, I reckon this is the answer to everyone\'s confusion. I\'m not saying it makes sense to so publicly nuke stimulus talks right before an election, but this is the thought process, erratic as it may be."</p><p>Another possibility, suggested by Chris Hayes, is that Trump may not be sending these tweets. Or perhaps he sent the "True!" tweet but not the other. That may be possible, and may explain the apparently disordered thinking, but it raises yet another terrifying possibility: Why are conflicting messages coming from the president\'s tweets? Foreign leaders read these tweets, and sometime the president issues military commands from Twitter. There should be no ambiguity about who is speaking from his account.</p><div class="around-the-web"><div class="from-your-site__headline">From Your Site Articles</div>\n        <ul </div></div><div class="widget__head"><a href="https://www.nationalmemo.com/ballot-drop-box"  aria-label="California Republicans Continue To Purloin Ballots In Illegal Drop Boxes">\n                                    data-runner-img-md="https://assets.rebelmouse.io/eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpbWFnZSI6Imh0dHBzOi8vYXNzZXRzLnJibC5tcy8yNDUxMDE3My9vcmlnaW4uanBnIiwiZXhwaXJlc19hdCI6MTYwNjU2NTIxOH0.BovrLPhrwzLuUe6siEjXoLo6zoH2n1sotiN6WZ4D4Yo/img.jpg?width=1245&coordinates=0%2C32%2C0%2C33&height=700"\n                                    data-runner-img-sd="https://assets.rebelmouse.io/eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpbWFnZSI6Imh0dHBzOi8vYXNzZXRzLnJibC5tcy8yNDUxMDE3My9vcmlnaW4uanBnIiwiZXhwaXJlc19hdCI6MTYwNjU2NTIxOH0.BovrLPhrwzLuUe6siEjXoLo6zoH2n1sotiN6WZ4D4Yo/img.jpg?width=980"\n class="lazyload-placeholder">\n                                    <div class="runner-spinner">\n                                      <svg class="runner-spinner-circular" viewBox="25 25 50 50">\n                                        <circle class="runner-spinner-path" cx="50" cy="50" r="20" fill="none" stroke-width="3" stroke-miterlimit="10"/>\n                                      </svg>\n                                    </div>\n                                </div></div>\n                            </a>\n                </div><div class="widget__body clearfix sm-mt-1"><div class="photo-caption">\n        <p>An illegal drop box operated by California\'s Republican Party</p>\n    </div><div class="photo-credit">\n        \n    </div><div class="body js-expandable clearfix js-listicle-body js-update-url css-listicle-body-2648221017"\n        \n            data-elid="2648221017"\n            data-post-url="https://www.nationalmemo.com/ballot-drop-box"\n            \n                data-authors="Tana Ganeva"\n            \n            \n                data-headline="California Republicans Continue To Purloin Ballots In Illegal Drop Boxes"\n            \n        ><div class="body-description" ><div class="inarticle_ad_placeholder" data-aa-adunit="/5931858/NatMemo_RM/NatMemo_Middle_Desktop_1" data-aaad="true"></div>\n<!--script id="3d14008d7e044c36b256c61ff82728bb">\nif(cnxFlag){\n\n  cnx.cmd.push(function() {\n    cnx({\n      playerId: \'5573e7ba-804a-4971-a00f-3e2eeec6c0a9\'\n    }).render(\'3d14008d7e044c36b256c61ff82728bb\');\n  });\ncnxFlag=false;\n}\n</script--><p>Despite a cease-and-desist order from California\'s Secretary of State, the state\'s Republican party continues to deny wrongdoing after setting up <a href="https://americanindependent.com/california-republicans-illegal-ballot-drop-boxes-voting-2020-election-secretary-of-state-alex-padilla/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">multiple illegal ballot drop boxes</a> around the state.</p><p>Law enforcement discovered the drop boxes \xe2\x80\x94 some of which were falsely labeled "official" \xe2\x80\x94 over the weekend.</p><p>On Monday, California Secretary of State Alex Padilla said that the operation was a clear breach of election law.</p><p>On Wednesday, Republican officials <a href="https://www.cbsnews.com/news/california-ballot-drop-boxes-republicans-cease-and-desist/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">falsely claimed</a> that their unofficial ballot drop boxes don\'t violate state law, and said they would continue to put up the fake drop boxes.</p><p>"There is nothing illegal about the collection of ballots provided by voters, on a certainly volunteer basis, and entrusted to the persons who are operating that local election, or local party office, from transmitting those ballots," California Republican Party general counsel Tom Hiltachk said.</p><script id="3d14008d7e044c36b256c61ff82728bb">\nif(cnxFlag){\ncnxFlag=false;\n  cnx.cmd.push(function() {\n    cnx({\n      playerId: \'5573e7ba-804a-4971-a00f-3e2eeec6c0a9\'\n    }).render(\'3d14008d7e044c36b256c61ff82728bb\');\n  });\n}\n</script><p>"We\'re going to continue with the program because it complies with the law," he added.</p><p>Padilla said many of the ballots found in the drop boxes were invalid because they were missing information, such as the identity of the person submitting the vote and their relationship to the voter.</p><p>Donald Trump has routinely accused his adversaries of exploiting official state drop boxes to tamper with ballots, which he <a href="https://www.nytimes.com/2020/09/24/us/politics/trump-republicans-election-transition.html" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">has called</a> "a whole big scam."</p><div class="inarticle_ad_placeholder" data-aa-adunit="/5931858/NatMemo_RM/NatMemo_Middle_Desktop_2" data-aaad="true"></div>\n<div class="video-container" id="videoCont" style="display: none;"></div>\n<div id="vid"></div><p>"Some states use \'drop boxes\' for the collection of Universal Mail-In Ballots," Trump <a href="https://twitter.com/realdonaldtrump/status/1295385113862090753" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">tweeted</a> in August. "So who is going to \'collect\' the Ballots, and what might be done to them prior to tabulation? A Rigged Election? So bad for our Country. Only Absentee Ballots acceptable!"</p><p>There is <a href="https://www.cbsnews.com/news/california-ballot-drop-boxes-republicans-cease-and-desist/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">no evidence</a> for this claim. Official ballot boxes are designed to ensure the security and integrity of individual ballots.</p><p>This is just the latest example of Trump working to undermine the legitimacy of the presidential election that former Vice President Joe Biden is <a href="https://projects.fivethirtyeight.com/2020-election-forecast/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">favored to win</a>.</p><p>The Trump campaign has filed a <a href="https://www.brennancenter.org/our-work/court-cases/voting-rights-litigation-2020" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">flurry of lawsuits</a> mostly targeting blue states to make it more difficult to vote safely during the COVID-19 <a href="https://fivethirtyeight.com/features/five-ways-trump-and-gop-officials-are-undermining-the-election-process/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">pandemic</a>.</p><p>Meanwhile, Republicans across the country continue to uphold restrictive voter ID <a href="https://fivethirtyeight.com/features/five-ways-trump-and-gop-officials-are-undermining-the-election-process/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">laws</a> and other laws that make it harder for citizens to vote.</p><p>In Texas, a three-judge panel <a href="https://americanindependent.com/texas-ballot-drop-boxes-trump-judges-greg-abbott/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">upheld</a> Republican Gov. Greg Abbott\'s decision to limit each county in the state to just one official ballot drop box. The judges who ruled in the case were all appointed by Trump.</p><p>As Nov. 3 inches closer, Trump will likely continue to try to sow confusion and invalidate the election\'s results ahead of time.</p><p>Last month, a reporter <a href="https://www.nytimes.com/2020/09/24/us/politics/trump-republicans-election-transition.html" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">asked Trump</a> if Americans could expect a peaceful transition of power if Biden wins the election.</p><p>"We\'re going to have to see what happens, Trump replied.</p><p><em>Published with permission of The American Independent Foundation.</em></p><div class="around-the-web"><div class="from-your-site__headline">From Your Site Articles</div>\n        <ul class="around-the-web__list"><li class="from-your-site__item">\n                        <a href="https://www.nationalmemo.com/texas-gov-abbott-orders-new-vote-suppression-measures" class="from-your-site__link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Texas Gov.
